font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">祁怡元：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盼成的朋友。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月和张盼成一样祁怡元在自行录制的视频上公开表示反对一党专政、要求言论自由和释放“被失踪”公民等。随后遭当局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，<span lang="EN-US"> 90</span>后民主青年祁怡元、张盼成因言获罪案已经宣判。因言获罪，祁怡元、张盼成分别被北京西城法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。祁怡元刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钱采芹： </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，江苏省无锡、宜兴两市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余维权人士来到宜兴市拘留所迎接两会期间被行政拘留的维权人沈方明出狱，不料他已被其辖区派出所提前接走，随后大家前往沈方明的家中为他接风洗尘。事后，当大家前往火车站查看返程车次时，却遭到大批特警的抓捕。目前已知，其中任美娇、钱采芹、夏建妹、周友良、汤永斌、王培成<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钱风林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张家口法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，钱风林女士在康保县县城张文营街上送法轮功台历时，遭国保大队吕正带人抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午，遭庭审。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，钱风林被康保县法院一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金一万元。钱风林不服判决，上诉到张家口中级法院。上诉被驳回。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">强巴格勒</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县尼措寺僧人，现年<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁，是道孚县人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日傍晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点多钟，强巴格勒在前往附近一佛塔转经途中，突然被中共公安人员拘捕。被指在僧舍中挂有西藏国旗，并曾表露想要为西藏政教事业而自焚的念头。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">强巴旺秋（藏）</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">:1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区边波隆都县索托乡（注：此为藏语拼音名，汉语地名不明，疑为拉萨市附近某县<span lang="EN-US">/</span>乡）人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Jampel Wangchuk</span>，俗名次培（<span lang="EN-US">Tsephel</span>），拉萨市哲蚌寺洛色林僧院高级僧人、纪律纠察僧官，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺所在僧侣学院进修学习；后因长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim&nbsp; Rinpoche</span>），成为其身边主要弟子，随拥有深厚博学的藏传佛学知识，且被哲蚌寺洛色林僧院确定为高级僧人及纪律纠察僧官；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，西藏发生大规模以僧侣为主体的抗议示威活动，以表达对中共当局长期压制、管控藏区人民的不满；他们强烈呼吁中共当局要实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并要求让达赖喇嘛回国返乡，对藏区进行自治管理等政治诉求；针对此，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，拉萨的哲蚌寺约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦本着推动实现这些诉求，发起进一步的大规模抗议活动，使事态迅速波及到整个拉萨市区，甚至四川及青海藏区；对于此次抗议行动，中共警方随即采取了制止行为，但又因中共手段过于极端，导致双方发生对峙冲突，期间部分僧人被抓；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被拉萨市警方突然以涉嫌“抗议活动”刑拘，自此失联；另有同寺僧侣好友贡觉尼玛、阿旺觉尼亦被拘捕；后其被拉萨市警方正式逮捕，理由是虽未参加当时的抗议示威，但因未能阻止所在寺庙僧人举行大规模抗议行动，遂属于违规或违反相关管理条例行为；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，终被拉萨市中级法院秘密重判无期徒刑，罪名不详；据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，至今其在狱中健康状况及所处具体环境等均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔娜然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省衡水市安平县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午，乔娜然遭到安平县公安绑架，被关押到衡水看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日得知，乔娜然被安平县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南新郑市法轮功信徒、残疾人。家住新郑市龙湖镇沙窝李村，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午被新郑市警方以“扫黑除恶”的名义抓捕，家中私人物品被掠走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，新郑市法院对乔向阳判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦来宾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南商丘网友，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日傍晚被警方约谈，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被控涉嫌寻衅滋事刑事拘留，羁押在商丘市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日遭正式逮捕，其家人透露被捕原因是在推特发贴攻击国家领导人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被商丘市睢阳区法院以寻衅滋事罪由判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有期徒刑，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日转送周口西华监狱服刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦艳秋<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省太仓市法轮功学员。原是苏州太仓邮政局职员，曾经<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被绑架迫害，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并被关过精神病院六个月迫害。她丈夫石泽惠曾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次被绑架，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被判刑两次共<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，秦艳秋被太仓<span lang="EN-US">610</span>国保警察绑架。同时被绑架的法轮功学员还有董美英与陈永林。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦艳秋、董美英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦永敏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，湖北省鄂州市籍人，早年为湖北省武汉钢铁公司冷轧厂职工，著名民间政治学者、自由撰稿人，中国民主党湖北省党部重要创始人，“中国人权观察”（注册中）理事长、“玫瑰中国团队”负责人，著名人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被湖北省当局再度非法抓捕，罪由是“接受外媒采访及写文章过多”，其妻亦遭当局拘押、失联；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日获悉，其已被湖北省武汉市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密羁押。现得知被羁押于武汉市第二看守所，案子在检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日第一次获律师会见，状态良好。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午在武汉中级法院三号审判庭公开宣判。秦永敏被以颠覆政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日止。</span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">覃德富：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省人，基督徒，成都秋雨圣约归正家庭教会长老，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>成都秋雨教案当事人之一，中国在押良心犯。近年来受洗皈依基督教，后在成都秋雨圣约家庭教会当长老；因与牧师王怡等众神职人员及信徒多次在成都市街头宣传基督教福音，并坚持其所在教会以“家庭教会”模式为主聚会，拒绝参加中共认可的“三自教会”，遂遭中共当局严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其在<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">9</span>秋雨教案大抓捕中被成都市青羊区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被以“非法经营罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">覃永沛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西人权律师。覃永沛是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被注销律师牌照。由他主持，曾代理过不少维权案件的”百举鸣律师事务所”，被勒令解散后，转为法律咨询公司的形式，继续提供法律服务。覃永沛也连同多名维权律师，成立“中国律师后俱乐部”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月末，覃永沛所属原律师事务所律师陈家鸿被玉林警方拘留，罪名为“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。当时覃永沛曾积极作出声援及呼吁放人，目前陈家鸿律师尚在羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日傍晚五点左右，南宁警方十数人闯入原百举鸣律师事务所（现百永鸣法律咨询服务有限公司）办公室，将该所原主任、人权律师后覃永沛控制并带走，同时覃的办公室被警方查封。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛被指涉煽动颠覆国家政权罪遭刑事拘留。现关押在南宁第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邱汉浓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省河源市东源县船塘镇六十多岁的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，东源县公安局国保大队警察闯到法轮功学员邱汉浓家，抄家、抢劫。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午六点多钟将邱汉浓抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并勒索罚钱<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">裘小平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁，湖南长沙人，上世纪八十年代初应召入伍，曾参与”对越自卫反击战”，退伍后被分配到长沙某国有企业工作。除了个人的劳动纠纷，身为退伍军人的裘小平亦积极参与老兵维权活动，多次参与各地老兵维权群体事件以及其他公民维权活动，因此招致长沙当地维稳部门的记恨。裘小平于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬由长沙前往北京维权，在国家人社部等相关部门递交了申告材料后，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日自行返回长沙，在走出长沙火车站时被一早等候的长沙芙蓉区朝阳街道工作人员及朝阳派出所警察等维稳人员强行带走，在做完相关笔录后即被宣布行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，罪名是“寻衅滋事”和“非法上访”。裘小平拘留届满，警方将裘小平转为刑事拘留，罪名不变，由拘留所转押长沙市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，裘小平案在湖南长沙市芙蓉区法院开庭审理，并被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">全世欣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，北京维权人士、推友。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，全世欣于被海淀警方带走，下午全世欣所在村委会告诉前来询问情况的全的好友，全世欣已被海淀警方刑事拘留，罪名为“寻衅滋事”，羁押在海淀区看守所。去年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，全世欣也曾被控在推特上“抨击党和国家领导人”被以寻衅滋事处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原公民、网络活跃人士，网名婷婷。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日遭太原警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事为由刑事拘留，目前关押在太原第三看守所。著名媒体人潇男女士介绍说：婷婷参与了微信群不计其数的公益讲座转播，她为中国民间社群的思想交流，奉献了上千个日夜，她勤勉、低调、勇敢，她是最富志愿者精神的网络义工之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲嘉唯色（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏拉萨市林周县人，林周县旁多村村民，生态环境保护者，村民维权代表，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年以来，中共当局以资源开发为由，一直在西藏拉萨市林周县旁多乡进行“旁多水利枢纽工程”建设，为防止反对声音，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召集当地藏民开会，强调该工程因是中共高层指令，若有藏人反对，就将以政治罪名论处；然而，随着相关部门施工工作的运作，不仅在当地进行长时间的测量、建桥及建路等，还接连不断的在旁多村和宁布村一带炸山挖石，肆意开采矿产，导致当地生态环境严重受损，同时附近民房出现裂痕、大面积农田被毁坏；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，该水利枢纽工程正式开工，当局宣称自同<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日起试运行后，该工程“将对增强城市防洪和改善城乡供水能力、改善生态环境等发挥巨大的作用”，但此一举却引来其家乡村民的十分不满，并称当局是以建设水利工程为名，行掠夺资源之实；与此同时，曾因当局多次强迫其家乡旁多村<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>人）藏民整村搬迁，随引起藏民的集体反对；其作为村民维权代表，曲嘉唯色与他人多次前往当地管理部门投诉请愿，但无任何效果，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被迫再次发起请愿游行，以期借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但却遭到中共军警的残酷镇压，包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名村民维权代表被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曲嘉唯色等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人请愿游行案在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由分别重判<span lang="EN-US">8-12</span>年不等刑期，曲嘉唯色亦被秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲桑嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海省海南藏族自治州安多茫拉县鲁仓寺僧人曲桑嘉措，带领当地一民间组织，长期向农牧民们提供藏文化教育方面的帮助。他于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日遭中共当局拘捕，至今下落不明。今年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底曲桑嘉措就曾因他所撰写的一些文章内容，而遭当局拘押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，而此次遭捕至今，他的家属仍未被告知他的被捕原因。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">R</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">热合江•再努拉（哈萨克）、热杂提•热斯汗（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任凤妹、任美娇、任胜林、任素香、任秀英、任志强、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日赛（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">荣春成、荣西（藏）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">如凯•嘎玛桑珠（藏）<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">热杂提﹒热斯汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，新疆昌吉市回族自治州奇台县人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，昌吉回族自治州奇台县五马场哈萨克乡清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人）。因其在乡里面为一死者做祷告，并按宗教习俗进行祷告仪式下葬，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年遂被当地警方以“宣扬极端宗教思想”为由抓捕，后被秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在被判刑之后，又被当作打击宗教极端思想的典型案例，强刮胡子，将其五花大绑，象文化大革命一样在奇台县游街示众。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任凤妹：上海市法轮功学员。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，上海市虹口区广中路派出所警察伙同虹口区国保警察闯入任凤妹家中，非法抄走了家里一台电脑主机、二台打印机、多份资料，并将任凤妹非法关押在虹口区看守所。一个月内都没有给过家属一张被关押的通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，任凤妹被批捕。上海市静安区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午非法对善良法轮功学员任凤妹判刑三年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任美娇：<span lang="EN-US"> 2</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，江苏省无锡、宜兴两市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余维权人士来到宜兴市拘留所迎接两会期间被行政拘留的维权人沈方明出狱，不料他已被其辖区派出所提前接走，随后大家前往沈方明的家中为他接风洗尘。事后，当大家前往火车站查看返程车次时，却遭到大批特警的抓捕。目前已知，其中任美娇、钱采芹、夏建妹、周友良、汤永斌、王培成<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任胜林：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多岁，四川省德阳市人，原德阳市什邡市钻釆厂退休工人，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰和宣传法轮功而长期受到什邡市当局的监控打压。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被四川省什邡市回澜镇派出所警方突击传唤，并被非法送到什邡市拘留所拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点，再次被便衣警察非法绑架，其家被查抄，搜走大量有关法轮功书籍和资料宣传品，后被以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，他被什邡市法院一审以“组织实施邪教罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前仍被关押在德阳市公安局监管中心。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任素香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区元宝山镇南庙村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十五岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，赤峰市元宝山区公安局多个警察非法闯入任素香的家，抢走打印机、电脑、现金等私人物品。当时任素香到邻居家，警察追到邻居家将她抓捕。任素香被关押在元宝山区看守所。在这没有任何法律程序的情况下，任素香被构陷到法院。法院指派的律师不仅不维护任素香的权利，还威胁任素香与她家人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日任素香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任秀英（哈尔滨）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任志强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">著名退休企业家、公众人物。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因言获罪而遭强迫失踪。据信应和他近期的关于武汉疫情应追究习近平责任的言论有关。任志强以大胆敢言著称，深受网民追捧。在愈来愈蔓延的疫情下，中共当局不但不反省自己的失职与无能，反而变本加厉的封口堵嘴，近日连党内著名人士任志强也遭强迫失踪，其如此行径及至丧心病狂，令全世界唾弃和鄙视。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，遭强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个半月的任志强因言获罪遭开除党籍并被正式抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日赛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1983</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人予以重判，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等措施；在此情况下，日赛所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方刑拘，并以涉嫌“参与抗议示威” 、“秘密组织相关人员在昂扎家里参加会议”等罪由被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，具体罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">荣春成</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早上被李家营派出所警察抓捕，被关押在高密看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">荣西（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村村民，原籍为四川甘孜州德格县，现年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，妻子名叫央吉，无子女。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。目前情况不名。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">如凯•嘎玛桑珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，西藏自治区贡觉县人，藏族，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年度“西藏自治区劳动模范”，原嘎玛国际生态文化发展有限公司董事长、西藏天珠之路文化传播有限公司董事长、青海三江源生态环保发展有限公司董事长、东方收藏家协会和自然之友会员等，著名古董商，慈善家，环保人士，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其致力于文化与环境保护工作，曾多次获得政府颁发的相关奖项；曾为家乡建桥梁修学校、抚恤孤寡老人；曾成立著名的三江源生态环境保护协会，并从事文物收藏保护；曾创建天珠之路文化传播有限公司，并多次与省级博物馆进行合作；曾与中国藏学研究中心达成协议，准备将<span lang="EN-US">200</span>件珍藏的文物捐献给国家等等，被央视电台提名为<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年度慈善家；本为模范中国公民，之后却因得罪地方当局而备受牢狱之灾。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年，因其在不知情的前提下购买了总值为<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>美金的七世纪古董毯、刺绣枕垫与鞋子等被盗古墓物品，随被巴州警方以涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”于同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日刑拘，后经查证其对被窃之物确系毫不知情，且其拥有正规的买卖古董许可证，遂于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又因同一罪名被拘，之后又以同一理由于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被正式解除取保候审。但十年之后旧事重提，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，第三次因涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”被西藏自治区若羌县警方刑拘，被关押在新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县法院以“盗掘古墓葬罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。现在新疆阿克苏地区的沙雅监狱服刑；据悉，在审讯期间曾多次遭遇酷刑，致其左耳几近失聪，双目视力模糊。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">S.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">萨尔克提江（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赛坎•汗巴尔（哈萨克）、赛尔克•叶热克西（哈萨克）、赛尔克•叶热西克、塞力克江·阿德勒汗（哈萨克）、塞努拜尔·吐尔逊（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">桑珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">色力克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>木海（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沙阿呆提·巴吴顿（维）、沙部旦•沙伊合（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">单丽娜、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">单珊、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尚恺、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盛杰、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">施凤兰、施凤香、施根源、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石玲、石香云、石雪梅、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">史桂芝、史在河、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">时宁瑶、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">释道果、释宗才、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵长华、邵承洛、邵重国、邵明亮、邵秀艳、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈滨、沈力、沈良庆、沈顺荣、沈忠勤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">申利清、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋桂香（青岛市）、宋国礼、宋开友、宋孔华、宋霞、宋玉洁、宋玉芝、宋志刚、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏东亮、苏恒、苏坤、苏瑞琴、苏士杰、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南次帕（藏）索南达夫（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南公保（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南林珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙桂昌、孙俊、孙林、孙平、孙茜、孙永耀、孙志芬、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">萨尔克提江（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆昌吉市人，吉昌市木垒县哈萨克族双语中学教师，网络作家，异见人士。因其亲友在哈萨克斯坦或和土耳其国生活，其持护照到土耳其与其亲友有过会面，因而引起新疆中共地方当局的敏感与紧张。当他回国后，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年某月即被极差自治州警方刑拘，后被正式批捕，指控其“带父母和岳母前往土耳其和哈萨克斯坦国，在当地见了流亡海外的反华哈萨克人”，又指他在木垒县哈萨克族中学非法从事宗教活动，宣扬非法宗教等。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右被昌吉市法院以莫须有罪名秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赛坎<span lang="EN-US">.</span>汗巴尔（哈萨克）：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆阿勒泰市人，阿勒泰市喀拉希力克乡<span lang="EN-US">Zhalchi </span>牧场<span lang="EN-US">3</span>小队村民，哈萨克族良心犯。因被新疆当局指控他在微信群与哈萨克斯坦亲友频繁联系，宣扬、传播宗教极端思想等，所以于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被阿勒泰市警方抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，他已被当地法院以不知名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赛尔克·叶热克西（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县萨尔布拉克镇开里木库拉村二组人，哈萨克族，阿拉木图州常驻居民，萨尔布拉克镇某清真寺阿訇，哈萨克国绿卡持有者，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，因中共当局对国内各少数民族（尤其是维吾尔族、哈萨克族、回族、藏族、蒙古族等）区域百姓采取高压严控政策，遂大量民众试图以出国留学、海外旅游探访、移民申请及获取绿卡等方式寻求更加自由民主的生存空间，而此举立刻引发了中共当局的极端不满与恐惧，故而各少数族裔民众，从政治异见人士，维权人士及人权捍卫者，公共知识分子，清真寺阿訇及寺庙僧侣、喇嘛，政府职员及各层级高官，普通公民等，均被视为维稳打击的对象；近年来，又因新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克斯族等民众常去的国家被中共政府视为反共基地或不友好国家，新疆安全部门故列出<span lang="EN-US">26</span>个中亚等国名单，排名第一的国家是土耳其和哈萨克斯坦共和国，一旦发现有少数民族人士欲到名单上的国家探亲或留学，立即被建立秘密档案，甚至禁止出国和抓捕判刑；赛尔克·叶热克西因已持有哈萨克共和国绿卡，并获取哈国政府“归国侨民证”，同时，正在办理哈国移民手续，随遭严密监控和肆意打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被地方警方抓捕，并被送乌鲁木齐市“去极端化培训学校”接受思想再教育；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又被转送到伊宁县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被伊犁哈萨克族自治州霍城县法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，罪名不详。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赛尔克﹒叶热西克：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆伊犁哈萨克族自治州霍城县萨尔布拉克镇一清真寺阿訇。在已经获得哈萨克斯坦共和国政府“归国侨民证”的情况下，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被新疆公安抓到位于乌鲁木齐的“去极端化培训学校”接受所谓的再教育，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬，又被转送到伊宁县看守所。据悉，阿訇赛尔克﹒叶热西克已获得过哈萨克斯坦国绿卡，其家中有母亲、妻子和三个孩子。他的一个姐姐已于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年移民哈国并加入哈国国籍，现住在阿拉木图，母亲与二姐、弟弟在阿斯塔纳定居。赛尔克﹒叶热西克的家人曾多次向霍城县公安局查询，但当局答复称“无可奉告”。其被捕前曾表示，等刚出生的第三个孩子拿到护照后，就会移民哈萨克斯坦。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">塞力克江·阿德勒汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，伊犁哈萨克自治州新源县塔德勒镇喀尔哈勒村公民，伊犁哈萨克自治州霍尔果斯市对外陆路口岸劳务运输工，中国在押良心犯。被抓捕前，曾一度在新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州霍尔果斯市对外贸易（陆路）口岸从事劳务及运输工作，为人安分守己，遵纪守法；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，突然被伊宁市警方从霍尔果斯市口岸莫名带走刑拘，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被伊宁市检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕，被指控因其在口岸工作期间，劳务输出工作曾被政府监控部门拍录，因而被认定大有“非法经营”之嫌；但其家人坚称，其被抓捕主要原因在于其姐移民国外，并自愿放弃中国国籍而成为哈萨克共和国公民，故其被作为打击报复对象所致；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案在伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市法院两次庭审， <b><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，终被一审以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</b>目前被羁押于伊犁哈萨克自治州伊犁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">塞努拜尔·吐尔逊（维）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，出生年月不详，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州伊利市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Sanubar Tursun</span>，著名维吾尔族歌唱家和木卡姆歌者，国际乐坛知名维吾尔族音乐人，素有“维吾尔族歌后”之称，中国在押政治犯。因出生于新疆伊犁知名的音乐世家，自幼即开始学习木卡姆（民族特有唱法，属于世界非物质文化遗产）、民歌和都塔尔乐器等；早年曾就读于新疆艺术学院扬琴专业，毕业后在新疆木卡姆艺术团工作，担任歌唱、创作等各项工作，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年又考入上海音乐学院作曲系学习作曲；自<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年至其被捕之前，曾出版发行<span lang="EN-US">10</span>张唱片、创作百余首歌曲，并出版了《赛努拜尔歌曲》一书；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾在美国和意大利出版了其演唱的木卡姆和新疆民歌的唱片；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，其首张国际唱片《希望》因收录了伊犁传统民歌及其自创歌曲，被意大利一家知名音乐唱片公司在全球发行；因其高超的音乐天赋和技艺，多年来其歌曲倍受海内外推崇欢迎，并曾受邀于土耳其、伦敦、巴黎等多个城市举办演唱会；然而，近年来，因中共当局加强了对新疆的严管控制，其歌曲尽管表达了维吾尔族人无法公开表达的感情，然因其编写歌词谨慎，注意不超越当局所设界限，故而其音乐会倍受万人瞩目，但其受欢迎程度却令中共当局深感不安；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其定于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月在法国雷恩、昂热和南特的演出被当局突然取消，其出行明显受到限制，不久即被失踪，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其家人终获消息，知其早已被捕，疑先送“教育转化”营地（实指集中营）进行思想及“伊斯兰极端主义”信仰改造，后被新疆伊犁市中级法院秘密庭审，被以不知名罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>月；据悉，至今当局一直拒透其具体下落何在。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">桑珠（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村领导，年过<span lang="EN-US">40</span>，多年来担任玛多县扎陵湖乡第六大队领导，后担任扎陵湖乡河源新村领导。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">色力克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>木海（维）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆塔城地区沙湾县一清真寺伊玛目（领祷人）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被捕后，被关于政治再教育营，至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沙阿呆提·巴吴顿（女）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Shaadaiti bawudun</span>，原伊犁州伊宁市伊犁饭店职工，中国在押良心犯。被捕前从未参与过政治维权或请愿活动，为人忠厚老实，深得子女的热爱；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾与丈夫海米提·阿不都热合曼到土耳其旅行，并与流亡瑞典，经常参与政治维权的儿子托格鲁克·海米提见过面，此时其子已获取在瑞典的政治庇护身份；但其返回新疆后，因当时新疆尚未出现“政治再教育营”之说，故其行踪虽被当局知晓，但并未被伊宁市警方问讯或传唤训诫，就此其夫妇二人一直相安无事；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，随着中共当局在新疆出现大规模清理少数民族宗教文化行动以来，新疆各地越来越多的推行“政治思想再教育营”（又称“政治再教育中心”）计划，其曾经出国旅游探亲之举（即曾与成为瑞典政治难民的儿子见面），即刻使其变成当局敌对仇视和需要打击报复的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其与丈夫二人被伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市警方双双带走，并被送当地“政治再教育中心”培训、关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，知其在“政治再教育营”接受强制洗脑培训<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年之后，又被伊宁市警方以“与在海外申请政治庇护的儿子会面”为罪由转为正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，沙阿呆提·巴吴顿和丈夫海米提·阿不都热合曼都被伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市法院一审以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日；据悉，看守所羁押期间，其身体情况极差；其在乌鲁木齐市银行（银联）工作的女儿因其被抓，亦于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被强送“政治再教育中心”接受洗脑式教育，至今下落不明。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沙部旦•沙伊合（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">单丽娜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省阜新市法轮功学员。一个五十几岁的善良妇女，原本拥有一个普通的小家庭，残疾的丈夫离不开她的悉心照顾，在外地读书的孩子离不开她的经济与精神的支持，而今只因她信仰法轮功而遭遇迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，阜新市海州公安分局国保大队闯入单丽娜家中无理抄家，抢走打印机、电脑等私人财物，同时抓捕了单丽娜。单丽娜因身体出现病态，几经周折后由丈夫接回家。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被拘捕至阜新市新地看守所，<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在新地看守所被非法开庭，<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并勒索罚款五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">单珊：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚上，单珊和法轮功学员田丰及蒋立宇，在北京街头张贴揭露“天安门自焚假案”的不干胶贴纸，被非法抓捕关押至今。据大陆媒体报导，蒋立宇、田丰及单珊分别被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尚恺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（笔名佣耕）中国亲毛泽东网站“红色参考”编辑部编辑，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以“寻衅滋事”的罪名刑拘。 “红色参考”编辑部人员涉嫌鼓动大学生前往深圳声援佳士工运，被指是幕后推手。据大陆传媒界人士披露，“红色参考”编辑部北京办公室涉嫌呼吁北京等地的大学生，前往广东声援佳士科技公司工人，并向工人提供资金。此事令广东高层震怒。于是决定在上周五采取联合行动，在北京警方的协助下，广东国保对“红色参考”编辑部及人员，采取搜查及拘捕行动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盛杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市旅顺法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，大连政法委策划，采用手机监控、跟踪、定位、蹲坑等手段，在大连地区各县区同一时间统一行动，抓捕了数十名法轮功学员，有很多人当天被放回，有的当月回家，最后还有多人被判刑。这次抓捕被公安国保称为“<span lang="EN-US">1614</span>”大案。刘仁秋、盛杰、谷树春、王红玉四名法轮功学员，被旅顺法院二次非法开完庭后，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下判决书， 刘仁秋被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚款五万元；盛杰<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半、罚款三万元；王红玉<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚金款三千元。盛杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">施凤兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。施凤香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">施凤香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">54</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。施凤香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">施根源（网名：断代工程）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被福建警方以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，关进福建泉州看守所，推特号被注销。之后<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被批捕，涉嫌罪名是寻衅滋事。施根源（断代工程）因在网络发表和传播“断代工程”言论，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘捕，后在泉州国保暗示下，家属配合做了精神病学鉴定，并于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日获释，但这个鉴定却成为施根源<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月再度身陷囹圄的陷阱。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚从家中被当地警方强行带走，后发现被警方送进泉州市精神病院（市第三医院），事件从头至尾均未经家属同意或签字确认。后获释。施根源此次又因推特言论遭逮捕，这是一起典型的以言治罪的案件。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被福建泉州市丰泽区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员石玲，女，约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>来岁，家住渝北区加州。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日上午，石玲在江北区蚂蝗梁散发法轮功资料时被抓捕，随后警察即到其家搜查。现在石玲被非法关押在江北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体;
