font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石雪梅</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石雪梅与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周育琴、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石雪梅被冤判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，并处罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元（刑期至</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2025</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日）；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">史桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江法轮功学员赵兴有，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁，和老伴史桂芝，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁，家住黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区水泉乡。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，双城房产一工作人员去赵兴有夫妇所居住的水泉乡赵家村一村民家，给该村民的房屋拍照，发现赵兴有夫妇家的院墙上喷写有“法轮大法好”的字样，此工作人员心生恶念，把字样拍照下来，传给双城区公安局、六一零。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，警察将赵兴有夫妇抓捕。送哈尔滨做身体检查后，因史桂芝身体不合格，被放回家，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所，关押六天放回。放回后，指使保人监视他们，不准往墙上写字、不准去炼功点、不准接触修炼人等。后双城公安局警察将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇构陷到哈尔滨市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，法院法逮捕通知书，水泉乡派出所苏永生等又将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇再次绑架，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所非法关押，史桂芝因检查身体不合格放回。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，史桂芝再次被非法抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月上旬，赵兴有被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，史桂芝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。史桂芝被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱，赵兴有被劫入哈尔滨市呼兰监狱。史桂芝刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">史在河：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省信阳市潢川县法轮功学员。史在河，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，家住潢川县黄寺岗镇史寨村，普通农民。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被信阳市潢川县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并勒索处罚金二万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">时宁瑶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。时宁瑶刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">释道果（原名张超）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生人，法名释道果，山东枣庄维权人士，早年在北京务工期间觉醒，多年致力于网络民主理念宣传，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年因给在京维权人士发提醒搜捕信息被关押<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天，后剃度出家云游四海，修行、研究佛学期间依然不忘网络启蒙和落难同道救助，以致每有落脚寺庙即被驱逐。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年张超的女儿考入大学后，他希望能把女儿送出国外，以脱离当局的摆布。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日张超预定了往返德国的机票，欲前往考察了解情况。但在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日张超突然遭到枣庄市山亭分局的抓捕，随即被以涉嫌寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">释宗才：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，江苏省武进市人，佛教徒，常州市知名法师，法名“廓仪”（早期）<span lang="EN-US">/</span>“寂光”（现在），俗名张仲才，江苏省常州市三圣禅寺住持（又称方丈），维权僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年出家为僧以来，曾在上海佛学院进修研习，后又至江西省云居山真如禅寺受戒，在江苏省江阴市长泰庙发愿；<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年曾积极修建江阴市五灵寺，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年又开始修复常州市鸡龙山三义庙（现已更名为三圣禅寺），<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年曾到北京市法源寺求法；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，曾历任常州市武进佛协秘书长，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年至今，被选为佛协副会长<span lang="EN-US">12</span>届常州市武进区政协委员，故此，其一直堪称为佛教知名僧侣；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其所在寺庙遭遇常州市武进宏运有机化工有限公司在一墙之隔的地方强行埋设排污管网，为维护寺庙正当权益，其于次日向当地环保局、宗教局电话投诉，希望能得到尽快处理，但投诉无果，施工方（宏运化工公司）仍继续违规施工，无奈之下，其随亲自上前阻止施工；因众僧人与施工方、在场的警察等人发生冲突，且其在冲突中将对方挖掘机操纵杆掰下，遂被当地警方迅速以“故意毁坏公私财物”为由悉数予以传唤，后又被警方以涉嫌“妨碍公务罪”刑事拘留，后被常州市经济开发区检察院转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案被检察院以涉嫌“妨碍公务罪”、“职务侵占罪”移送常州市经济开发区法院起诉，截至目前，已正式进入法院审理环节。释宗才目前被羁押于常州市武进区看守所（常州市武进区广电东路<span lang="EN-US">99</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">213000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵长华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省丹东市振安区法轮功学员、女。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，邵长华因坚持信仰曾两次遭冤狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。期间在辽宁女子监狱，邵长华遭曾受到了超过人的极限的酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，邵长华被丹东国保及丹东八道派出所多个警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，邵长华被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵承洛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁，男，山东省青岛市城阳区流亭赵村人，中医针灸医生，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功而被青岛市当局多次绑架迫害，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在山东王村劳教所和山东省男子监狱时，曾遭受上百种酷刑，手指被强行折断，左脚大趾被砸断。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，邵承洛和妻子高文淑在夏庄镇发法轮功宣传材料时，被当地治安人员告发，随即被夏庄派出所警方以涉“邪教罪”抓走，当天傍晚其家被查抄，之后又被三次抄家，在没有出具任何凭据的情况下，劫走家里二万元现金及许多物品。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，城阳区法院在城阳看守所内设法庭，邵承洛及妻子高文淑被非法庭审，当庭未予宣判。之后其家人为妻子高文淑聘请了律师，律师向法官索杰提出再次庭审的要求，但遭拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇二人被山东青岛城阳区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别宣判：邵承洛被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、高文淑被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。其不服，已提起上诉。目前被关押在青岛市城阳看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵重国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，山西省运城市人，山西省运城市盐湖区槐豫东路新建二巷兴农社家属院居民，推特名“<span lang="EN-US">@</span>都市放牛娃”，职业不详，民主公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邵重国曾因在微信群“亡共倒计时”里发贴贬斥、批评中共时任国家领导人习近平，而被运城市警方处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因为民主公民子肃公开信代写资料，又被运城市警方处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因去陕西省佳县探访友人高智晟（注：高智晟当时虽已刑满释放，但仍被严控于陕北窑洞家中），而被陕西省榆林市警方知晓后抓捕、刑拘，并被关押在陕西省佳县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被陕西省佳县检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被检察院以同罪由提起公诉，指控其在推特上发信息贬斥中共当局及国家领导人习近平，于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，家属称其因涉“高智晟事件”而被陕西省佳县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，并且在看守所期间曾受到虐待（如被打、不准吃饭及不给提供卫生用品等）；后刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又被山西省运城市警方莫名抓捕，后得知被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，至今不予释放。目前羁押于山西省运城市看守所。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵明亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南京民运人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，邵明亮在南京被失踪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，律师获准进入看守所，与邵明亮见面约一个多小时。邵明亮请律师传告家人自己精神和健康状况尚好，追求民主宪政的信念与主张非常坚定！邵明亮被无辜抓捕，欲加之罪名 “寻衅滋事”。目前邵先生没有遭到刑讯和虐待的迹象。邵明亮一生无故挨打、关精神病院，撒传单遭遇车祸，成了残废人。财物身份证被扣留，被长期关押在响塘村家里，禁止出门购买食物、生活用品，禁止就医。邵明亮一直说：他们想我死，但我要活着，我不会自杀的，如果我死了，就是被迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邵秀艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，邵秀艳在汽车厂的岱山公园门口打电话时，被长春市公安局国保大队警察、经开七区派出所警察绑架。随后警察对她家进行非法抄查，抢走师尊法像、一套法轮大法书、一百多本《共产主义的终极目的》、三百元左右真相币、两部手机。邵秀艳被长春市公安局国保大队绑架后，被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，邵秀艳被公诉，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月末到宽城区法院，面临被庭审。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈滨：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，出生不详，原四川省彭州市彭白铁路局职工，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年以来，因信仰、宣传法轮功备受当局打压迫害，曾数次被非法拘留、劳教、关精神病院、洗脑班，并因此被迫流离失所近<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底，曾因信仰法轮功被非法劳教，在劳教所里曾遭虐待及长期包夹酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月在被非法劳教后，其所在公职单位将其无故除名、断绝生活来源，其户籍和身份证也被当地派出所违法注销。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾被非法绑架到精神病院进行迫害，同年下半年在精神病院被迫害成腰椎骨折，瘫痪在床，因绝食抗议而遭受“灌食”迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日再次被什邡市洛水镇警方绑架并抄家搜走计算机、打印机、塑封机、光盘刻录设备等大量私人物品，次日被以涉“邪教罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被什邡市法院以邪教罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其不服，已当庭提出上诉。目前被关押在德阳市公安局监管中心。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈力：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓洪成、肖兵、王军、李南海（火焱）、丁岩、王威、王建华、黄安阳、李江鹏等广东深圳<span lang="EN-US">10</span>公民遭抓捕。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后连续遭拘捕或强迫失踪。后警方向追寻下落的邓洪成、王军家属证实其已被羁押，被指涉颠覆。后被告知指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈良庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽著名异议人士沈良庆<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日遭合肥公安以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。现在被羁押在合肥看守所。沈良庆系安徽合肥人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁。中国著名异议人士，曾任职于安徽检察院。早在<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年，他便投身民主运动，创办民间刊物《大学生与社会》，宣扬自由人权与普世价值。因早年参与<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年被合肥法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被判刑一年半。 沈良庆刚直不阿，敢说敢言，常年在<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>上针砭时弊。六四大屠杀<span lang="EN-US">30</span>周年前夕，抓捕著名异议人士沈良庆是当局进一步封杀言论行动的一部分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈顺荣：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被上海市政府驻京办截访人员乘<span lang="EN-US">1461</span>列车送回上海的上海维权人士沈顺荣、席妫华夫妇被上海市公安局闸北分局北站派出所警察从府村路<span lang="EN-US">500</span>号黑监狱接到北站派出所，当晚被构陷“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈忠勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省沈阳市沈河区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日去沈北新区蒲河镇大集买东西，刚到那里不一会儿，被辉山派出所警察殴打绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被沈阳市沈北新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">申利清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北张家口市宣化区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日讲真相时，遭人恶告，被宣化区南关派出所警察绑架、抄家，并拘留十天。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，宣化区南关派出所通知申利清的家人，说已将申利清转为刑事拘留。申利清被非法关押到张家口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午九点河北张家口市宣化区法院对法轮功学员申利清庭审。律师依法从法律、道德和修炼的角度多方位有理有据的做了无罪辩护。最后律师和申利清一致要求无条件释放。未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋桂香（青岛市）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东青岛市胶州七旬法轮功学员。因信仰被迫害多年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，宋桂香及家人通过快递分别向北京最高检察院、最高法院邮寄了刑事控告书，控告江泽民发起对法轮功学员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，以阜安派出所负责人想找她们母女“谈话”的名义将宋桂香、李雪骗至派出所，然后羁押于青岛普东看守所进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，宋桂香被胶州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。因身体原因宋桂香于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日保外就医回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月又被送往山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋国礼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省白银市靖远县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。靖远县东湾镇三合村农民，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月修炼法轮功。因张贴法轮功标语，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，宋国礼在公交车上被靖远县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>绑架。后宋国礼被送到靖远县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被白银法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金八千元，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被送到甘肃省大沙坪监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋开友：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与唐祖琼、王应龙都是</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川宜宾珙县罗渡乡维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2OO5</span>年，宜宾在罗渡苗族自治乡、曹营乡、洛表镇共计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个村采取每个村社长代表村民签字的手法，占用<span lang="EN-US">2400</span>多村民的<span lang="EN-US">148.5525</span>公顷土地修建罗渡水电厂。他们降低地价，降低土地类别不按政策赔偿。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，罗渡水电站放炮损坏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个村<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多户村民房屋，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余户震成危房，未合理赔付。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，村民们再次找乡政府要求退回土地，巨浪公司代表周天柱指使<span lang="EN-US">42</span>人手持砍刀，把黄桷六社社员吴仪清打昏厥，送医院抢救，两天才苏醒致耳聋。此后村民一直在上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>号，四川宜宾珙县罗渡乡党委书记张强邀请<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名移民代表，前往珙县信访局商谈解决村民蹲守罗渡电站一事，村民代表进入后半小时，当局出动<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余特警等从现场抓走宋开友、唐祖琼、高英、王应龙、罗顺银<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，并以破坏生产经营罪刑事拘留，关押于宜宾大邑看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，珙县警方以破坏生产经营罪逮捕宋开友、唐祖琼、王应龙三人，并以“检察院不批捕，需要继续侦查”为由，决定高英、罗顺银<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人监视居住获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋孔华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋孔华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省抚顺法轮功学员四十多岁的宋霞女士，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被抚顺县嘉禾派出所警察绑架，被关押抚顺南沟看守所。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，宋霞案件移送到抚顺县检察院<span lang="EN-US">,</span>欲继续迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋玉洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省丹东市访民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚上，辽宁省辽阳市访民王静和辽宁省丹东市访民宋玉洁，在北京市大兴区六合庄住处被辖区大兴分局北臧村派出所抓捕，送交地方公安接回，王静被辽阳带回后平安回家，而宋玉洁被丹东带回后被关进看守所。此前，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">40</span>分，辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，这些人强行将<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的张正廷截回辽宁丹东，以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留。张正廷的爱人宋玉洁说，地方政府之所以截人，是因为自己拒绝接受政府提出的给予<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元人民币的维稳补助费，要求在“六四”敏感日前回丹东所致。到<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张正廷被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋玉芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。宋玉芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省葫芦岛市兴城市人，兴城市农机修造厂职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因手机丢失，被他人拾到后送到公安局，公安局发现他的手机中存有与法轮功有关的内容，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆阿克陶县公安局拘捕，后被阿克陶县检察院以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”批捕，并被关押在阿克陶县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被新疆阿克陶县法院以同罪名枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏东亮</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，前陕西省府谷县法院书记员、民事审判第一庭助审员，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年毕业于西北政法大学之后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，在陕西省府谷县法院参加工作并任书记员；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，任民事审判第一庭助理审判员，此期间，一直对现行司法体系的混乱与腐败等问题感到悲凉和无奈，并积极寻求如何改变社会问题的民主之路；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，他毅然辞去原有工作，前往广州等地参加民主活动，并与张六毛、项逢选等人结为好友，经常参与围观声援、同城聚餐等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、项逢选等多人一同被广州市珠海区警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘。一个月后被广州天河区检察院以涉“危害国家安全罪”正式批捕，并被定性为“制造炸弹危害公共安全案”主犯之一；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，获悉与其同案的维权公民张六毛在广州第三看守所被酷刑致死，而依然毫无信息，其家人亦因受官方恐吓而拒绝与外界联系。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，其可能已与项逢选一起被广州市中级法院以“危害国家安全案主犯”判刑。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏恒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东济宁人，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年苏参加高考，之后在东北的一所大学里就读了一年，当时感觉没意思，就退学到威海打工。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年回老家济宁，<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年去云南大理，<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月去了深圳。这次做工厂调查时，他的任职机构是在深圳的青草工友服务部，这个劳工<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>主要做工人热线<span lang="EN-US">(</span>咨询<span lang="EN-US">)</span>和工厂调查。苏恒因为做华坚工厂劳工调查被控非法使用窃听窃照设备器材罪被刑拘，目前在关押赣州市看守所。苏恒在会见时说：在看守所又提审了五次，包括最近的<span lang="EN-US">6.8</span>和<span lang="EN-US">6.15</span>的两次。这些提审主要集中在<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、拍摄手表的来源，拍摄的次数，内容和处理。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、他这次入厂调查有什么特别的目的，也提到了华坚厂为美国总统特朗普女儿伊万卡生产贴牌产品。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、跟李强的关系。苏恒说，经过这一个月的入厂调查，他认为在违反劳动法和血汗工厂方面，华坚厂要比珠三角的民营企业严重。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏坤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市尚志市苇河镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而屡遭中共<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室严厉逼迫打击。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，当二人与法轮功学员革振华一起坐着微型面包车去哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被恶人告发，回来的路上在亚布力镇，被赶来的当地警方围堵抓捕，前挡风玻璃被打碎，车辆被扣押，次日即被警方以涉邪教罪刑事拘留。同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日二人被转正式逮捕，同时关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案件被尚志市检察院向尚志市法院提起诉讼，并提出对革振华、苏坤冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年，对王翠娥冤判<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年的建议。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，二人被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别枉法重判：苏坤被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万，王翠娥被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。二人不服，提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，经哈尔滨市中级法院二审重新改判：苏坤被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万，王翠娥被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。据悉，关押期间，整整有半年时间，其家人均无任何他们的消息，知道后也不许家里人接见、只叫存钱，不许带进物品，庭审也没有通知家属。最终，<b>苏坤刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，</b>王翠娥刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏瑞琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">法轮功学员，家住秦皇岛市海港区，女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十七岁。法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被东环路派出所警察绑抓捕，警察抄走许多资料，并扬言说正赶上扫黄打黑点子上了。苏瑞琴的老伴是团级干部，去年去世。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏士杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省保定市清苑区东吕乡北宋村维权人士，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁。因宅基地纠纷被当地警方非法拘禁而多次上访，之后乡政府迫于苏士杰上访压力给予困难补助，事后起诉苏士杰敲诈政府，以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日将其从家中带走并逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，开庭审理一次，未让家属旁听，至今未判决未放人。现羁押于保定市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南次帕（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏昌都地区八宿县人，青年作家，曾在定日县经商。曾因持有达赖喇嘛尊者法像而两次入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，索南次帕就曾被冠上“危害国家安全罪”而被判两年徒刑；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，他再次被当局指控“撰写煽动民族矛盾文章、散发达赖喇嘛法像、破坏社会稳定”等，在拉萨遭关押一个月左右，并被处以罚款。索南次帕于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19&nbsp;</span>日在西藏首都拉萨再次遭当地公安拘捕，这是<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年以来第三次遭到中共公安的拘捕。目前亲友仍不清楚索南次帕被捕的原因，以及关押地点等情况。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南达夫（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，藏族，中国在押政治犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，不准挂达赖喇嘛头像等，引发多地藏民强烈不满；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，四川省甘孜州炉霍县僧俗藏人亦举行大规模和平示威游行，要求西藏自由，信仰自由，并高呼达赖喇嘛万岁等口号，随即遭到中共警方的武力镇压和大规模抓捕，警民冲突升级；最终导致多人被打死打伤，上百藏人在当时及随后被抓或失踪，数十人被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月至无期徒刑不等的刑期；索南达夫本人也因积极参与抗议示威活动，被警方以“聚众闹事”、 “参与炉霍县抗议示威和严重影响公共秩序的非法聚集”以及与境外势力有染等为由抓走，后被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以同罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南公保（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新吧龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Solnam Gonpo</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">索南林珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：索南林珠，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判无期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙桂昌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市中山区人，大连市热电公司职工，法轮功学员，良心犯。孙俊因是张霞的丈夫，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日下班后发现家被抄，就到青云小学询问，才知妻子已被民主广场派出所警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，孙俊到民主广场派出所询问妻子情况时也被警方扣押，后送姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，夫妇二人被中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，后被秘密开庭，最终被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审开庭即对他维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，孙俊被送往大连市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙林（孑木）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公民记者。男，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生在南京。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被南京<span lang="EN-US">18</span>频道录用，后因言语过激而被解聘，离开电视台。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月自己开办了一个“星梦影视制作中心”，由于被诬告被迫关闭。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被南京《今日商报社》录用，开办单独板块《大都市》任主编。同时也被“言语过激”而停刊。孙林是从<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月起，开始以“公民记者”的身份大量采访报道民间维权事件，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，南京的孙林和他太太何方在家中被警察带走，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，孙林被南京玄武区法院以<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法持有枪支罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，以<span lang="EN-US">"</span>聚众扰乱社会秩序罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，两罪并罚，合计执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日获释。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日在南京江宁区法院门口因围观王健涉嫌“寻衅滋事”案开庭，被警方带走。后经多方核实：孙林被关押在南京玄武区看守所，涉嫌罪名“聚众扰乱社会秩序”。后</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙林涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”一案圣诞节（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日）宣判，孙林获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省日照市法轮功学员，日照市裕华机械厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>两日，日照市公安局东港分局国保警察先后抓捕了法轮功学员公华、孙平、屈正蓉等八位大法学员，关押在日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日孙平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙茜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">加拿大华裔女富商。孙茜是北京利德曼生物化学公司的创始人，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年获加拿大国籍，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年登上胡润中国富豪榜，身家<span lang="EN-US">35</span>亿。由于操劳过度，身体严重透支，孙茜患上多种疾病，多方医治无效。在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年她学习炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙茜正在家中与表妹聊天，警方突然闯入抄家，搜出法轮功相关书籍后，将她抓捕。期间，孙茜多次遭受酷刑，被铐在铁椅子上，被辣椒水喷脸。全天被戴上镣铐，强制洗脑，强迫放弃她的信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孙茜一案在北京朝阳法院温榆河法庭开庭，孙茜获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙永耀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽阜南县基督教堂牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日中共当局强拆了安徽阜南县基督教堂，被强拆的安徽阜南县基督教堂可容纳<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多人并在礼拜，聚会时几乎座无虚席。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日下午，在没有任何合法的文件通知下遭到强拆，甚至教堂财物尽毁，来不及搬出。堂委会主任耿宜敏、牧师孙永耀于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点被以“涉嫌聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙志芬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。</span></div>
</div>
